 In this poster war, Nitish Kumar has also been targeted somewhere in the name of the government
 newjiland ke purv captain brendan maikulam ne kaha he ki vah match phixing maamle ko lekar apane purv saathi cricketer kris kerns ko kabhi maaf nahin karenge
 mccullum was a prosecution witness in the Cairns case
 landan kii ek adaalat ne haalanki pichley saal kerns ko sabhi aaropon se bari kar diya
 The comments is saal khel ko alavida kah chuke maikulam ne kaha kerns ke is daawey ke baad ki usne 2008 main match phixing ke liye unase sampark kiya tha, unhen laga ki gavaahi dena unki naitik jimmedaari he
 He told Radio New Zealand, 'but i felt that i am standing in the dock
 mere liye yah bahut kathin ho gaya tha
 i forgive easily and never mind
 main nahin chahta tha ki kerns ko jail ho or mujhe khushi he ki aisa hua bhi nahin
 He said, "I will never forgive him for his behavior though
" main ab usase koi matlab nahin rakhana chahta
 (apart from the headline, this news has not been edited by the NDTV team, it has been published directly from the Syndicate feed
 ) mccullum, who retired from the sport this year, said he felt it was his moral responsibility to testify after Cairns' claim that he had approached him for match-fixing in 2008
 unhone radio newjiland se kaha, 'lekin mujhe mahasoos hua ki main katghare main khadaa hum
 It was very difficult for me
 main aasaani se maaf kar detaa hum or kabhi man main koi baat nahin rakhata
 i didn't want Cairns to be jailed and I'm glad it didn't happen
 ' unhone kaha, 'main haalanki uske bartaav ke liye use kabhi maaf nahin karuunga 
 i don't want to make any sense to him now
 ' (hedline ke alaava, is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he, yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he
 ) (except for the headline, this news has not been edited by the NDTV team, it is published directly from the Syndicate feed
 ) Jat has been the Chief Minister of Haryana for two decades
 gair jat logon ko lag rahaa he ki is baar unki baari he
 An old journalist from Sonipat, covering all his experiences, said that Jat vs non-jat elections are being held this time
 congress or inelo jat netaa ke dam par lard rahe hai jabaki bijepi bina netaa ke gair jat matadaataaon ko samet rahi he
 Jat vs non Jat politics is not a new text in Haryana politics
 baat is par ho rahi thi ki kya bijepi gair jat banaam jaaton ke bich voton kaa dhruvikaran kar sakegi
 Since polarization is used in any other context in Indian politics, it would be better if we do not extract the meaning of polarization in those popular contexts here
 jab bijepi chautaala se lekar hooda ke bhrashtachar or gundai par hamale karti he to ek tarah se wo gair jat raajnneeti ko hi hawa de rahi hoti he
 In Haryana politics, MLA is more important than MP
 yahaan kii raajnneeti vidhayakon ke aas-paas gumti he
 It is a small state, but the politics of Ahirwal belt, Jat belt, GT road line goes through various divisive lines
 jaaton kii raajnneeti main malik jat samaaj kaa apana hi dabadabaa rahata he
 Malik Jats outnumber everyone in number and competence
 bijepi ne is baar malik khap ke pradhan dada balajit malik ko baroda vidhansabha se ummidavaar bana diya he
 The Malik Jat society has been divided into several parts about whether the head of the Khap should have taken a party ticket or not
 jat belt main malik jaaton kaa rujhaan bhi raajnneeti ko dhara badal detaa he magar is baar to mukhiya hi bijepi ke tikat par hai
 Dada Baljeet says that his grandfather had also contested the election of Punjab province before independence
 koi nai baat nahin he
 He named another Khap whose head is contesting the election
 dada balajit ne kaha ki saamaajik or raajnneetik kaam alag hote hai
 There is no big deal in this, but when i reached Bhainswal, a large and important village of Malik Jats, many people of Malik fraternity were questioning this
 unka kahana tha ki khap ke pradhan kii padavi mukhyamantri or vidhayak se bhi badi hoti he
 It should not be politicized
 isse pradhan kaa kad chota hua he
 Some people said that after they join BJP, we will choose a different Pradhan
 dada balajit se jab is bare main sawaal poocha to unhone kaha ki yah pad to vanshanugat he
 How can there be another leader? bijepi ne behad chaturaai se malik khap main bahes kii vibhaajan rekha khinch di he
 The maximum divide between Jats will benefit BJP because if their votes remain with Congress or go from Congress to INLD, then BJP may suffer
 jat bantenge to gaiyr jaaton ko laabh milegaa
 Seven BJP mps have been elected
 inamen se chah gaiyr jat birdari ke hai
 The bjp's only MP is a Jat
 pichhali vidhansabha main bijepi ke paas chaar vidhayak the
 So the party has nothing to lose
 wo har jagah badhati hui sunai de rahi he
 Old Ghagh discussants are also giving equal importance to the INLD to the BJP in their discussions
 agar bijepi gaiyr jat dhruvikaran main safal rahi to uski sarkaar banegi yaa bijepi ke bina kisi kii sarkaar nahin banegi
 Instead of giving leadership at the Haryana level, the BJP has divided its leaders region-wise
 pradhanmantri narendra modi or bijepi adhyaksh amit shah haryana main dhuandhar reliyaan kar rahe hai
 With the belief that if another rally takes place, another seat will emerge
 valmiki jayanti ke din pradhanmantri kii rohtak main raily thi
 He targeted Chief Minister Hooda that Dalit girls are not safe in the Chief Minister's area
 modi 2002 kii anusuchit jati janajati ayog kii report kaa bhi zikr kar rahe the ki 19 ladakiyon ke saath dalit hinsa hui he
 The Prime Minister is referring to the 12-year-old report that worked so hard to add one vote each
 shaayad uske baad koi report hi na ai ho, lekin isse bhi aage jaakar pradhanmantri ne dalit vot ko bijepi ke paale main karne ke liye jo roopak gadhe usase lagata he ki bijepi kitni rachanaatmak hoti ja rahi he
 She is creating new symbols every day and if she does not have it, she is grabbing it from someone else
 pradhanmantri ne rohtak raily main tirange kaa hawala dete hue kaha ki usamen sirf teen rang nahin he
 The Ashoka Chakra also has a blue color
 main chaar rang kii kranti laana chahta hum
 The saffron revolution, on hearing its name, causes fever to my secular friends
 wo so nahin pate hai
 Saffron means energy to people
 logon ko bijli chahie
 When have you heard such smart use of symbols in Indian politics in the last twenty years
 kitni aasaani ne pradhanmantri ne kesaria ko bhagava arth main dharmik pratik se nikaalkar bijli se jod diya
 The interpretation of the colors of the tricolor does not stop at saffron
 ve kehete hai ki safed kranti laaungaa
 Milk production will increase in the country
 harith kranti laaungaa
 We also need a blue revolution
 or neeli kranti kya he
 Modi says there is a need to increase the power of the sea so that we can strengthen the ports and encourage the fishermen
 neeli kranti ke naam se modi ne haryana ke daliton ko hi nahin machuaaron ko hi baat karne kaa ek mudda to de hi diya
 Very few people will know that Haryana is one of the top states in fisheries
 baaki dalon ke netaaon ke bhaashan ko suniye
 There are only attacks
 raajnneetik pratikon kaa istemaal nahin dikhegaa
 Perhaps they do not have the ability to do all this
 neeli kranti kaa naam lekar unhone haryana main chunaav ladane kii aupchaarikta nibhaa rahi mayawati kii neend to uda hi di hogi
 In the UP elections, see what flowers Modi feeds with this blue color
 haryana se bijepi kaa ek dalit saansad bhi he
 Who does not understand Mayawati's politics in Haryana? party kaa kisi se gathbandhan nahin he
 More Dalit voters than in UP are free to go anywhere
 mukhyamantri ke liye brahman ummidavaar tay kar mayawati ne haryana ke liye ek aupchaarikta puri kar di he
 There is no intense fight
 congress ke paas dalit adhyaksh he magar ashok tanvar kii saamaajik raajnneetik pahchaan banane kii prakriya main he
 At least they are not the identity of Dalit politics
 kahin gurjar to kahin dalit to kahin brahman to kahin punjabi har tarah ke samudaayon ko aage badhaakar bijepi apni daavedaari badhaati ja rahi he
 His propaganda is not only aggressive but his publicity is seen everywhere
 janata bhale yah tay nahin kar pai ho ki kise vot den magar is kanfusion main laabh bhi bijepi ko milegaa
 Congress is not making aggressive claims
 inelo takat se chunaav lard rahi he magar om prakaash chautaala ke kaaran nae matadaataaon, mahilaon or madhyamvarg main pakad nahin bana paa rahi he
 This is the reason that BJP will get so many seats on the strength of urban voters that no government will be formed without it
 kya pataa usee kii ban jaae
 Especially after the surrender of Om Prakash Chautala, the INLD will be affected
 inelo jitani kamazor hogi bijepi ko utana hi laabh hoga
 The INLD has made a mistake talking about running the government from jail
 tippaniyan Many people say that the result will be hung
 kuch kehete hai ki bijepi kaa gaanvon main sanghathan nahin he
 The organization had nowhere to go but brought more than 272 seats in the Lok Sabha
 iskaa kaaran he bijepi kaa chunaav abhiyaan
 Its intensity and intensity is so fast that it gets first in the eyes of the voters who never decide what to do
 sirf itnaa hi nahin bijepi ne chunaav ke samay duusari partiyon se sirf netaa hi nahin liye, balki un chote-mote netaaon ko bhi bula liya, jo sthaneey str par saamaajik pakad rakhte hai
 Critics may call them mercenary leaders, but the BJP has put its own awning on them
 isiilie vah charchaaon main number van par he
 Well, BJP does not have a chief ministerial candidate, but those who have it, why are they such a big name today that they can turn Haryana politics around them
 janata ke saamne naam kaa to sankat he hi nahin

 is aalekh main di gai koi bhi soochna athwa tathy athwa vyakt kiye gaye vichaar enditivi ke nahin hai, tathaa enditivi unke liye kisi bhi prakaar se uttaradaayi nahin he
 Dada Baljeet said that social and political work are different
 isamen koi badi baat nahin hai, lekin jab main malik jaaton ke ek bade or mahatvapurn gaanv bhenswaal pahunchaa to malik birdari ke kai log is baat par sawaal kar rahe the
 He said that the rank of the head of the Khap is greater than the Chief Minister and the MLA
 iskaa raajnneetikaran nahin karnaa chahie
 Due to this the height of the head has been reduced
 kuch logon ne kaha ki unke bijepi main jane ke baad ham alag pradhan chunenge
 When asked questions about this, he said that this post is hereditary
 koi doosraa pradhan kaise ho saktaa he
 The BJP has very cleverly drawn the dividing line of debate in Malik Khap
 jaaton ke bich zyada se zyada vibhaajan bijepi ko laabh milegaa kyonki agar inkaa vot congress ke paas rah gaya yaa congress se nikal kar inelo ke paas gaya to bijepi ko nuksaan ho saktaa he
 non-jats will benefit if the Jats are divided
 bijepi ke saat saansad chune gaye hai
 Six of them belong to non-jat community
 bijepi kaa ek hi saansad jat he
 The BJP had four mlas in the previous assembly
 isliye party ke paas khone ke liye kuch nahin he
 She is heard growing everywhere
 puraane ghaagh charchaakaar bhi apni charchaaon main bijepi ko inelo ke baraabar yaa usase bhi zyada tavajjo de rahe hai
 If BJP is successful in polarizing non-jats, it will form a government or no government will be formed without BJP
 bijepi ne haryana ke str par netritv dene ke bajaae apane netaaon ko ilakaur baant diya he
 Prime Minister Narendra Modi and BJP President Amit Shah are holding rallies in Haryana
 wo is vishwaas ke saath ki ek or raily ho jaae to ek or seat nikal aegi
 The Prime Minister had a rally in Rohtak on Valmiki Jayanti
 unhone mukhyamantri hooda par nishaanaa saadhaa ki mukhyamantri ke ilaake main dalit ladkiyaan surakshit nahin hai
 Modi was also referring to the 2002 report of the Scheduled Castes and Tribes Commission that there has been Dalit violence with 19 girls
 ek ek vot jodne ke liye itani mehnat kii pradhanmantri 12 saal puraani report kaa zikr kar rahe hai
 There may not have been any report after that, but even further, the metaphor that the Prime Minister coined to bring the Dalit vote to the bjp's court shows how creative the BJP is becoming
 wo har din nae pratikon ko garh rahi he or uske paas nahin he to kisi or se hadap le rahi he
 Citing the tricolor at the Rohtak rally, the Prime Minister said that it does not have only three colors
 ashok chakra main nila rang bhi he
 i want to bring a revolution of four colors
 kesaria kranti jiskaa naam sunakar mere secular mitron ko bukhaar chadh jaataa he
 They do not sleep kesaria kaa matlab he logon ko urja
 People need electricity
 pichley bees saal main bhartiya raajnneeti main aapane kab pratikon kaa itnaa smart istemaal suna he
 How easily the Prime Minister removed saffron from the religious symbol in saffron and connected it with electricity
 tirange ke rangon kii vyakhya kesaria par hi nahin thaharti he
 They say that i will bring white revolution
 desh main doodh kaa utpaadan badhegaa
 i will bring green revolution
 hamen neeli kranti kii bhi zarurat he
 And what is the blue revolution
 modi kehete hai ki samudr kii shakti badhaane kii zarurat he taaki ham bandargahon ko majboot kar saken or machuaaron ko badhaava de sake
 In the name of blue revolution, Modi has given a point to talk to fishermen not only to the Dalits of Haryana
 bahut kam log jaanate honge ki machhlee paalan main haryana awwal rajyon main se ek he
 Listen to the speech of the leaders of other parties
 sirf hamale hai
 Use of political symbols will not be seen
 shaayad unamem ye sab karne kii kshamta nahin he
 In the name of the blue revolution, he must have woken up Mayawati, who was playing the formality of contesting elections in Haryana
 upi chunaav main dekhte hai modi is nile rang se kya-kya gul khilaate hai
 There is also a Dalit MP of BJP from Haryana
 haryana main mayawati kii raajnneeti kiske khilaaf he samaj hi nahin aata
 The party has no alliance with anyone
 upi se kahin zyada dalit matadaata aaazaad hai kisi bhi taraf jane ke liye
 Mayawati has completed a formalization for Haryana by deciding a Brahmin candidate for Chief Minister
 koi saghan ladaai nahin he
 The Congress has a Dalit president but is in the process of becoming the social political identity of Ashok Tanwar
 kam se kam wo dalit raajnneeti kii pahchaan to nahin hi hai
 Somewhere the Gujjars, the Dalits, the Brahmins, and the Punjabis, the BJP is increasing its claim by advancing all kinds of communities
 uskaa prachaar aakraamak to he hi balki usee kaa prachaar sab jagah dikhataa he
 The public may not be able to decide whom to vote for, but BJP will also get the benefit in this confusion
 congress aakraamak daavedaari kar nahin rahi he
 The INLD is contesting the elections with power, but due to Om Prakash Chautala, it is not able to hold new voters, women and middle class
 yahi sab kaaran he ki bijepi shahari matadaataaon ke dam par itani siten to hasil kar hi legi ki uske bina kisi kii sarkaar nahin banegi
 What should be his address? khaaskar om prakaash chautaala ke sarender karne ke baad inelo par asar to padegaa hi
 The weaker the INLD, the more the BJP will benefit
 inelo ne jail se sarkaar chalaane kii baat kar galati kii he 
 The comments kai log kehete hai ki nateeja trishanku hoga
 Some say that BJP does not have an organization in the villages
 sanghathan to uske paas kahin nahin tha, loksabhaa main 272 se bhi zyaada siten le ai
 The reason for this is the bjp's election campaign
 uski saghanta or tivrata itani tej hoti he ki wo un matadaataaon kii nigahon main sabase pehle chadh jaati he, jo kabhi tay nahin kar pate ki kya karen
 Not only this, BJP not only took leaders from other parties at the time of elections, but also called small leaders who have social hold at the local level
 aalochak inhen bhaade ke netaa kah sakate hai, magar bijepi ne inhen ke dam par apana shaamiyana laga liya he
 That is why he is at number one in discussions
 thik he ki bijepi ke paas mukhyamantri kaa ummidavaar nahin he magar jinke paas he kyon wo aaj itane bade naam hai ki haryana kii raajnneeti ko apane aas paas ghuma saken
 There is no crisis of name in front of the public

 jat bantenge to gaiyr jaaton ko laabh milegaa
 Seven BJP mps have been elected
 inamen se chah gaiyr jat birdari ke hai
 The bjp's only MP is a Jat
 pichhali vidhansabha main bijepi ke paas chaar vidhayak the
 So the party has nothing to lose
 wo har jagah badhati hui sunai de rahi he
 Old Ghagh discussants are also giving equal importance to the INLD to the BJP in their discussions
 agar bijepi gaiyr jat dhruvikaran main safal rahi to uski sarkaar banegi yaa bijepi ke bina kisi kii sarkaar nahin banegi
 Instead of giving leadership at the Haryana level, the BJP has divided its leaders region-wise
 pradhanmantri narendra modi or bijepi adhyaksh amit shah haryana main dhuandhar reliyaan kar rahe hai
 With the belief that if another rally takes place, another seat will emerge
 valmiki jayanti ke din pradhanmantri kii rohtak main raily thi
 He targeted Chief Minister Hooda that Dalit girls are not safe in the Chief Minister's area
 modi 2002 kii anusuchit jati janajati ayog kii report kaa bhi zikr kar rahe the ki 19 ladakiyon ke saath dalit hinsa hui he
 The Prime Minister is referring to the 12-year-old report that worked so hard to add one vote each
 shaayad uske baad koi report hi na ai ho, lekin isse bhi aage jaakar pradhanmantri ne dalit vot ko bijepi ke paale main karne ke liye jo roopak gadhe usase lagata he ki bijepi kitni rachanaatmak hoti ja rahi he
 She is creating new symbols every day and if she does not have it, she is grabbing it from someone else
 pradhanmantri ne rohtak raily main tirange kaa hawala dete hue kaha ki usamen sirf teen rang nahin he
 The Ashoka Chakra also has a blue color
 main chaar rang kii kranti laana chahta hum
 The saffron revolution, on hearing its name, causes fever to my secular friends
 wo so nahin pate hai
 Saffron means energy to people
 logon ko bijli chahie
 When have you heard such smart use of symbols in Indian politics in the last twenty years
 kitni aasaani ne pradhanmantri ne kesaria ko bhagava arth main dharmik pratik se nikaalkar bijli se jod diya
 The interpretation of the colors of the tricolor does not stop at saffron
 ve kehete hai ki safed kranti laaungaa
 Milk production will increase in the country
 harith kranti laaungaa
 We also need a blue revolution
 or neeli kranti kya he
 Modi says there is a need to increase the power of the sea so that we can strengthen the ports and encourage the fishermen
 neeli kranti ke naam se modi ne haryana ke daliton ko hi nahin machuaaron ko hi baat karne kaa ek mudda to de hi diya
 Very few people will know that Haryana is one of the top states in fisheries
 baaki dalon ke netaaon ke bhaashan ko suniye
 There are only attacks
 raajnneetik pratikon kaa istemaal nahin dikhegaa
 Perhaps they do not have the ability to do all this
 neeli kranti kaa naam lekar unhone haryana main chunaav ladane kii aupchaarikta nibhaa rahi mayawati kii neend to uda hi di hogi
 In the UP elections, see what flowers Modi feeds with this blue color
 haryana se bijepi kaa ek dalit saansad bhi he
 Who does not understand Mayawati's politics in Haryana? party kaa kisi se gathbandhan nahin he
 More Dalit voters than in UP are free to go anywhere
 mukhyamantri ke liye brahman ummidavaar tay kar mayawati ne haryana ke liye ek aupchaarikta puri kar di he
 There is no intense fight
 congress ke paas dalit adhyaksh he magar ashok tanvar kii saamaajik raajnneetik pahchaan banane kii prakriya main he
 At least they are not the identity of Dalit politics
 kahin gurjar to kahin dalit to kahin brahman to kahin punjabi har tarah ke samudaayon ko aage badhaakar bijepi apni daavedaari badhaati ja rahi he
 His propaganda is not only aggressive but his publicity is seen everywhere
 janata bhale yah tay nahin kar pai ho ki kise vot den magar is kanfusion main laabh bhi bijepi ko milegaa
 Congress is not making aggressive claims
 inelo takat se chunaav lard rahi he magar om prakaash chautaala ke kaaran nae matadaataaon, mahilaon or madhyamvarg main pakad nahin bana paa rahi he
 This is the reason that BJP will get so many seats on the strength of urban voters that no government will be formed without it
 kya pataa usee kii ban jaae
 Especially after the surrender of Om Prakash Chautala, the INLD will be affected
 inelo jitani kamazor hogi bijepi ko utana hi laabh hoga
 The INLD has made a mistake talking about running the government from jail
 tippaniyan Many people say that the result will be hung
 kuch kehete hai ki bijepi kaa gaanvon main sanghathan nahin he
 The organization had nowhere to go but brought more than 272 seats in the Lok Sabha
 iskaa kaaran he bijepi kaa chunaav abhiyaan
 Its intensity and intensity is so fast that it gets first in the eyes of the voters who never decide what to do
 sirf itnaa hi nahin bijepi ne chunaav ke samay duusari partiyon se sirf netaa hi nahin liye, balki un chote-mote netaaon ko bhi bula liya, jo sthaneey str par saamaajik pakad rakhte hai
 Critics may call them mercenary leaders, but the BJP has put its own awning on them
 isiilie vah charchaaon main number van par he
 Well, BJP does not have a chief ministerial candidate, but those who have it, why are they such a big name today that they can turn Haryana politics around them
 janata ke saamne naam kaa to sankat he hi nahin

 This is called virtual water trade under which if a country imports any agricultural produce, it is also importing the water to grow it, indirectly, because it would have to apply its own water for such produce

 isamen saaf taur par kaha gaya he ki koi bhi sarvice prowider contant main bhedbhaav nahin kar saktaa he
 If you do not know about Net Neutrality, then tell that it is a principal under which it has been decided that no Internet service provider shall discriminate all its customers in content
